Before diving into Genesis 6, let me briefly address your observation:
ğŸŒ¿ About â€œYahwehâ€ appearing differently:
In the Hebrew Bible, God is referred to by several names, and different sections emphasize different aspects:
 âœ… ×Ö±×œÖ¹×”Ö´×™× (Elohim) â†’ God as Creator, Ruler, Judge (power, majesty).
 âœ… ×™Ö°×”×•Ö¸×” (YHWH, Yahweh) â†’ God as personal, covenantal, relational; His revealed name to Moses in Exodus 3 (â€œI Am that I Amâ€).
 âœ… El Shaddai, El Elyon, Adonai â†’ additional titles reflecting specific attributes.
Genesis 6 marks a turning point where Yahwehâ€™s relational nature and Elohimâ€™s cosmic authority come together sharply.

âœ… Yahwehâ€™s Personal Visit â†’

âœ… The Cry of Sodom â†’

âœ… Abrahamâ€™s Intercession â†’

âœ… The Pattern of Divine Justice â†’

ğŸ“– Genesis 1 Reflection
